102→\t\tHandler: admission.NewHandler(admission.Create, admission.Update),\n   103→\t\t// TODO: enable this once we've swept secret usage to account for adding secret references to service accounts\n   104→\t\tLimitSecretReferences: false,\n   105→\t\t// Auto mount service account API token secrets\n   106→\t\tMountServiceAccountToken: true,\n   107→\n   108→\t\tgenerateName: names.SimpleNameGenerator.GenerateName,\n   109→\t}\n   110→}\n   111→\n   112→// SetExternalKubeClientSet sets the client for the plugin\n   113→func (s *Plugin) SetExternalKubeClientSet(cl the pod should be admitted\n   138→func (s *Plugin) Admit(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n   139→\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n   140→\t\treturn nil\n   141→\t}\n   142→\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n   143→\t\t// we only mutate pods during create requests\n   144→\t\treturn nil\n   145→\t}\n   146→\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n   147→\n   148→\t// Don't modify the spec of mirror pods.\n   149→\t// That makes the kubelet very angry and confused, and it immediately deletes the pod (because the spec doesn't match)\n   150→\t// That said, don't allow mirror pods to reference ServiceAccounts or SecretVolumeSources either\n   151→\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n   152→\t\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\t// Set the default service account if needed\n   156→\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) == 0 {\n err != nil {\n   162→\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"error looking up service account %s/%s: %w\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName, err))\n   163→\t}\n   164→\tif 168→\t\tpod.Spec.ImagePullSecrets = make([]api.LocalObjectReference, len(serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets))\n   169→\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets); i++ {\n   170→\t\t\tpod.Spec.ImagePullSecrets[i].Name = serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets[i].Name\n   171→\t\t}\n   172→\t}\n   173→\n   174→\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n   175→}\n   176→\n   177→// Validate the data we obtained\n   178→func (s *Plugin) Validate(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n   179→\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n   180→\t\treturn nil\n   181→\t}\n   182→\n   183→\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n   184→\n   185→\tif a.GetOperation() == admission.Update && a.GetSubresource() == \"ephemeralcontainers\" {\n   186→\t\treturn 239→\tif a.GetResource().GroupResource() != api.Resource(\"pods\") || (a.GetSubresource() != \"\" && a.GetSubresource() != \"ephemeralcontainers\") {\n   240→\t\treturn true\n   241→\t}\n   242→\tobj false\n   252→}\n   253→\n   254→func shouldAutomount(sa *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) bool {\n   255→\t// Pod's preference wins\n   256→\tif pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n *sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n   262→\t}\n   263→\t// Default to true for backwards compatibility\n   264→\treturn true\n   265→}\n   266→\n   267→// enforceMountableSecrets indicates whether mountable secrets should be enforced for a particular service account\n   268→// A global setting of true will override any flag set on the individual service account\n   269→func (s *Plugin)  278→\n   279→\treturn false\n   280→}\n   281→\n   282→// getServiceAccount returns the ServiceAccount for the given namespace and name if it exists\n   283→func (s *Plugin) getServiceAccount(namespace string, name string) (*corev1.ServiceAccount, error) {\n   284→\tserviceAccount, err := s.serviceAccountLister.ServiceAccounts(namespace).Get(name)\n   285→\tif err == nil 312→\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(api.Resource(\"serviceaccount\"), name)\n   313→}\n   314→\n   315→func (s *Plugin) limitSecretReferences(serviceAccount *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) envFrom referencing secret.secretName=\\\"%s\\\" is not allowed because service account %s does not reference that secret\", container.Name, envFrom.SecretRef.Name, serviceAccount.Name)\n   344→\t\t\t\t}\n   345→\t\t\t}\n   346→\t\t}\n   347→\t}\n   348→\n   349→\tfor _, container := range pod.Spec.Containers {\n   350→\t\tfor _, env := range container.Env {\n   351→\t\t\tif %s referencing secret.secretName=\\\"%s\\\" is not allowed because service account %s does not reference that secret\", container.Name, env.Name, env.ValueFrom.SecretKeyRef.Name, serviceAccount.Name)\n   354→\t\t\t\t}\n   355→\t\t\t}\n   356→\t\t}\n   357→\t\tfor _, envFrom := range container.EnvFrom {\n   358→\t\t\tif envFrom.SecretRef != nil {\n   359→\t\t\t\tif should enforce mountable secrets.\n\t// The value must be true to have this annotation take effect\n\tEnforceMountableSecretsAnnotation = \"kubernetes.io/enforce-mountable-secrets\"\n\n\t// ServiceAccountVolumeName is the prefix name that will be added to volumes that mount ServiceAccount secrets\n\tServiceAccountVolumeName = \"kube-api-access\"\n\n\t// DefaultAPITokenMountPath is the path that ServiceAccountToken secrets are automounted to.\n\t// The token file would then be accessible at /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount\n\tDefaultAPITokenMountPath = \"/var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount\"\n\n\t// PluginName is the name of this admission plugin\n\tPluginName = \"ServiceAccount\"\n)\n\n// Register registers a plugin\nfunc Register(plugins *admission.Plugins) {\n\tplugins.Register(PluginName, func(config io.Reader) (admission.Interface, error) {\n\t\tserviceAccountAdmission := NewServiceAccount()\n\t\treturn serviceAccountAdmission, nil\n\t})\n}\n\nvar _ = admission.Interface(&Plugin{})\n\n// Plugin contains the client used by the admission controller\ntype Plugin struct {\n\t*admission.Handler\n\n\t// LimitSecretReferences rejects pods that reference secrets their service accounts do not reference\n\tLimitSecretReferences bool\n\t// MountServiceAccountToken creates Volume and VolumeMounts for the first referenced ServiceAccountToken for the pod's service account\n\tMountServiceAccountToken bool\n\n\tclient kubernetes.Interface\n\n\tserviceAccountLister corev1listers.ServiceAccountLister\n\n\tgenerateName func(string) string\n}\n\nvar _ admission.MutationInterface = &Plugin{}\nvar _ admission.ValidationInterface = &Plugin{}\nvar _ = genericadmissioninitializer.WantsExternalKubeClientSet(&Plugin{})\nvar _ = genericadmissioninitializer.WantsExternalKubeInformerFactory(&Plugin{})\n\n// NewServiceAccount returns an admission.Interface implementation which limits admission of Pod CREATE requests based on the pod's ServiceAccount:\n// 1. If the pod does not specify a ServiceAccount, it sets the pod's ServiceAccount to \"default\"\n// 2. It ensures the ServiceAccount referenced by the pod exists\n// 3. If LimitSecretReferences is true, it rejects the pod if the pod references Secret objects which the pod's ServiceAccount does not reference\n// 4. If the pod does not contain any ImagePullSecrets, the ImagePullSecrets of the service account are added.\n// 5. If MountServiceAccountToken is true, it adds a VolumeMount with the pod's ServiceAccount's api token secret to containers\nfunc NewServiceAccount() *Plugin {\n\treturn &Plugin{\n\t\tHandler: admission.NewHandler(admission.Create, admission.Update),\n\t\t// TODO: enable this once we've swept secret usage to account for adding secret references to service accounts\n\t\tLimitSecretReferences: false,\n\t\t// Auto mount service account API token secrets\n\t\tMountServiceAccountToken: true,\n\n\t\tgenerateName: names.SimpleNameGenerator.GenerateName,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetExternalKubeClientSet sets the client for the plugin\nfunc (s *Plugin) SetExternalKubeClientSet(cl kubernetes.Interface) {\n\ts.client = cl\n}\n\n// SetExternalKubeInformerFactory registers informers with the plugin\nfunc (s *Plugin) SetExternalKubeInformerFactory(f informers.SharedInformerFactory) {\n\tserviceAccountInformer := f.Core().V1().ServiceAccounts()\n\ts.serviceAccountLister = serviceAccountInformer.Lister()\n\ts.SetReadyFunc(func() bool {\n\t\treturn serviceAccountInformer.Informer().HasSynced()\n\t})\n}\n\n// ValidateInitialization ensures an authorizer is set.\nfunc (s *Plugin) ValidateInitialization() error {\n\tif s.client == nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"missing client\")\n\t}\n\tif s.serviceAccountLister == nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"missing serviceAccountLister\")\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Admit verifies if the pod should be admitted\nfunc (s *Plugin) Admit(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n\t\t// we only mutate pods during create requests\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n\n\t// Don't modify the spec of mirror pods.\n\t// That makes the kubelet very angry and confused, and it immediately deletes the pod (because the spec doesn't match)\n\t// That said, don't allow mirror pods to reference ServiceAccounts or SecretVolumeSources either\n\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n\t\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n\t}\n\n\t// Set the default service account if needed\n\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) == 0 make([]api.LocalObjectReference, len(serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets))\n\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets); i++ {\n\t\t\tpod.Spec.ImagePullSecrets[i].Name = serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets[i].Name\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n}\n\n// Validate the data we obtained\nfunc (s *Plugin) Validate(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o \"ephemeralcontainers\" {\n\t\treturn s.limitEphemeralContainerSecretReferences(pod, a)\n\t}\n\n\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n\t\t// we only validate pod specs during create requests\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Mirror pods have restrictions on what they can reference\n\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n\t\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) != 0 {\n\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"a mirror pod may not reference service accounts\"))\n\t\t}\n\t\thasSecrets := false\n\t\tpodutil.VisitPodSecretNames(pod, func(name string) bool {\n\t\t\thasSecrets = true\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}, podutil.AllContainers)\n\t\tif hasSecrets {\n\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"no service account specified for pod %s/%s\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Name))\n\t}\n\t// Ensure the referenced service account exists\n\tserviceAccount, err := admission.NewForbidden(a, err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc shouldIgnore(a admission.Attributes) bool {\n\tif a.GetResource().GroupResource() != api.Resource(\"pods\") || (a.GetSubresource() != \"\" && a.GetSubresource() != \"ephemeralcontainers\") {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tobj := a.GetObject()\n\tif obj == nil {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\t_, ok := obj.(*api.Pod)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc shouldAutomount(sa *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) bool {\n\t// Pod's preference wins\n\tif pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n\t\treturn *pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n\t}\n\t// Then service account's\n\tif sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n\t\treturn *sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n\t}\n\t// Default to true for override any flag set on the individual service account\nfunc (s *Plugin) enforceMountableSecrets(serviceAccount *corev1.ServiceAccount) bool {\n\tif s.LimitSecretReferences {\n\t\treturn time.Millisecond\n\tfor i := 0; i < numAttempts; i++ {\n\t\tif i != 0 {\n\t\t\ttime.Sleep(retryInterval)\n\t\t}\n\t\tserviceAccount, err := s.client.CoreV1().ServiceAccounts(namespace).Get(context.TODO(), name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\treturn serviceAccount, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !errors.IsNotFound(err) {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(api.Resource(\"serviceaccount\"), name)\n}\n\nfunc (s *Plugin) limitSecretReferences(serviceAccount *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) error {\n\t// Ensure all secrets the pod references are allowed by the service account\n\tmountableSecrets := sets.NewString()\n\tfor _, s := range serviceAccount.Secrets {\n\t\tmountableSecrets.Insert(s.Name)\n\t}\n\tfor _, volume := range pod.Spec.Volumes {\n\t\tsource := volume.VolumeSource\n\t\tif source.Secret == nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tsecretName := source.Secret.SecretName\n\t\tif !mountableSecrets.Has(secretName) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"volume with secret.secretName=\\\"%s\\\" is not allowed because service account %s does not reference that secret\", secretName, serviceAccount.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, container := range pod.Spec.InitContainers {\n\t\tfor _, env := range container.Env {\n\t\t\tif env.ValueFrom != nil && envFrom.SecretRef.Name, serviceAccount.Name)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// limit pull secret references as well\n\tpullSecrets := sets.NewString()\n\tfor _, s := range nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Plugin) limitEphemeralContainerSecretReferences(pod *api.Pod, a admission.Attributes) error {\n\t// Require ephemeral container pods to have service accounts\n\tif klog.Logger, queue workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[T], key T, requeue bool, maxRetries int) {\n\tif !requeue {\n\t\tqueue.Forget(key)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\trequeueCount := queue.NumRequeues(key)\n\tif requeueCount < maxRetries {\n\t\tqueue.AddRateLimited(key)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"retried several times\", \"key\", key, \"count\", requeueCount)\n\tqueue.Forget(key)\n}\n\nfunc (e *TokensController) queueSecretSync(obj interface{}) {\n\tif secret, ok := obj.(*v1.Secret); ok ADMISSION CONTROLLER (plugin/pkg/admission/serviceaccount/admission.go): The ServiceAccount admission plugin implements MutationInterface and ValidationInterface. When a pod is created, the Admit() method checks whether to auto-mount the service account token by calling shouldAutomount(), which evaluates pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken and serviceAccount.AutomountServiceAccountToken fields (defaulting to true for backward compatibility). If auto-mounting is enabled, mountServiceAccountToken() adds volume mounts to all containers and creates a Projected volume with the TokenVolumeSource(), which includes: (a) ServiceAccountToken projection for the actual JWT token, (b) ConfigMap projection for the kube-root-ca.crt certificate, and (c) DownwardAPI projection for the namespace. These are mounted to /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount.\\n\\n2. TOKEN CONTROLLER (pkg/controller/serviceaccount/tokens_controller.go): The TokensController watches ServiceAccount and Secret resources to manage service account token secrets. When a pod's service account needs a token secret, the controller's generateTokenIfNeeded() method (called from syncSecret()) generates the actual JWT token using the Claims() function and stores it in the secret's data fields (token, ca.crt, namespace). The controller maintains the token secrets as service accounts are created, updated, and deleted.\\n\\n3. SERVICE ACCOUNTS CONTROLLER (pkg/controller/serviceaccount/serviceaccounts_controller.go): Creates default service accounts in every namespace via syncNamespace(). This ensures the 'default' service account exists, which can be referenced by pods that don't explicitly specify a service account.\\n\\nTOKEN GENERATION FLOW: The token generation pipeline (pkg/serviceaccount/claims.go and legacy.go) provides the Claims() function which creates JWT claims containing the service account identity, and optionally binds tokens to specific pods, secrets, or nodes. The LegacyClaims() function provides backward compatibility for legacy secret-based tokens. Both claim types are used by generateTokenIfNeeded() to create the actual JWT token string stored in the secret.\\n\\nPOD SPEC VALIDATION: The automountServiceAccountToken field is defined in pkg/apis/core/types.go for both PodSpec (allowing per-pod override) and ServiceAccount (setting namespace-wide default). The admission controller's Validate() method also enforces that pods have a valid service account reference and validates secret references based on the service account's mounted secrets list.\\n\\nThe complete pipeline ensures that: (1) pods automatically receive mounted service account tokens unless explicitly disabled, (2) tokens are stored as Kubernetes secrets, (3) token data is generated and managed automatically, and (4) service accounts exist in all namespaces.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":601,"cache_read_input_tokens":61275,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":601},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8fd2e003-2d1a-4624-8abc-9486e7f7a572","uuid":"114ed0b0-7aef-4a8c-bcbe-8836c25345ec"}
